            on bi1_0.bo_id=itm1_0.stock_in_boid 
    left join

            on bm1_0.bill_id=bi1_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi2_0 
            on bi2_0.bo_id=bm1_0.bo_id 
    left join

            on bi2_0.bo_id=bd1_0.bo_id 
    left join

            on bi1_0.bo_id=bd2_0.bo_id

            on su1_0.supplier_id=itm1_0.supplieruuid

            on csd1_0.id=su1_0.cust_sellerdetails_id

            on csi1_0.supplier_id=csd1_0.master_cust_seller_id 
    left join

            on pah1_0.bill_id=bt1_0.bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=pah1_0.bo_id 
    left join

            on bm3_0.bill_id=bi3_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=bd3_0.bo_id 
    where
        bt1_0.bo_id=?

            on itm1_0.stock_in_transactionuuid=bt1_0.in_transaction_model_stock_in_transactionuuid 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi1_0 
            on bi1_0.bo_id=itm1_0.stock_in_boid 
    left join
        bill_model bm1_0 
            on bm1_0.bill_id=bi1_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi2_0 
            on bi2_0.bo_id=bm1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd1_0 
            on bi2_0.bo_id=bd1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd2_0 
            on bi1_0.bo_id=bd2_0.bo_id 
    left join
        master_cust_seller su1_0 
            on su1_0.supplier_id=itm1_0.supplieruuid 
    left join
        cust_seller_details csd1_0 
            on csd1_0.id=su1_0.cust_sellerdetails_id 
    left join
        master_cust_seller csi1_0 
            on csi1_0.supplier_id=csd1_0.master_cust_seller_id 
    left join
        bill_model pah1_0 
            on pah1_0.bill_id=bt1_0.bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=pah1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bill_model bm3_0 
            on bm3_0.bill_id=bi3_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=bd3_0.bo_id 
    where
        bt1_0.bo_id=?

        master_bo_model bi1_0 
            on bi1_0.bo_id=itm1_0.stock_in_boid 
    left join

            on bm1_0.bill_id=bi1_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi2_0 
            on bi2_0.bo_id=bm1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd1_0 
            on bi2_0.bo_id=bd1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd2_0 
            on bi1_0.bo_id=bd2_0.bo_id 
    left join
        master_cust_seller su1_0 
            on su1_0.supplier_id=itm1_0.supplieruuid 
    left join
        cust_seller_details csd1_0 
            on csd1_0.id=su1_0.cust_sellerdetails_id 
    left join
        master_cust_seller csi1_0 
            on csi1_0.supplier_id=csd1_0.master_cust_seller_id 
    left join
        bill_model pah1_0 
            on pah1_0.bill_id=bt1_0.bill_id 
    left join
        master_bo_model bi3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=pah1_0.bo_id 
    left join
        bill_model bm3_0 
            on bm3_0.bill_id=bi3_0.bill_model_bill_id 
    left join
        bo_details bd3_0 
            on bi3_0.bo_id=bd3_0.bo_id 
    where
        bt1_0.bo_id=?
